policy-map NORTEL-REVA-QOS-POLICY

  police rate percent 20
   conform-action transmit
   exceed-action transmit
   violate-action drop
  !
  priority level 1
  queue-limit 256 packets
 !

  bandwidth percent 60
  queue-limit 64 packets

  bandwidth percent 3
  queue-limit 512 packets

  bandwidth percent 17
  queue-limit 64 packets
 !

  queue-limit 512 packets

  2001:4888:23f:6200::/56,
  2001:4888:2000:0:3a0:2a0::/112
end-set

  10.182.168.0/24,
  10.249.208.192/27,

  0.0.0.0/0,
  ::/0
end-set

  0.0.0.0/0
end-set

community-set LTE_COMMUNITIES
  6167:10998
end-set
!
route-policy LTE_IN
  if destination in BLOCKED_LTE_ROUTES_IN then
    drop
  elseif destination in LTE_ROUTES_IN then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy WDN_IN
  if destination in BLOCKED_WDN_ROUTES_IN then
    drop
  elseif destination in WDN_ROUTES_IN then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy LTE_OUT
  if destination in LTE_ROUTES_OUT then
    set community LTE_COMMUNITIES
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy WDN_OUT
  if destination in WDN_ROUTES_OUT then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy MLDP-INBAND
  set core-tree mldp-inband
end-policy
!
route-policy DENY_ALL_RIP
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy ADVERTISE_TO_CELL
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0, ::/0) then
    pass
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy RAN_REDIST_STATIC_TO_OSPF
  if tag is 190 then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
